} catch(e) {}\n  }\n  \n  globalSynth.cancel();\n  currentState = 'SPEAKING';\n  notifyListeners();\n  \n  const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n  utterance.rate = 1.0;\n  utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n  utterance.volume = 1.0;\n  \n  const voices = globalSynth.getVoices();\n  const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\n  if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n  \n  utterance.onend = () => {\n    console.log('[AgenticBar] Speech ended');\n    currentState = 'IDLE';\n    notifyListeners();\n    onDone?.();\n    \n    // Resume listening\n    if (wasRestarting) {\n      shouldRestart = true;\n      setTimeout(() => startListening(), 200);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  utterance.onerror = () => {\n    currentState = 'IDLE';\n    notifyListeners();\n    onDone?.();\n    if (wasRestarting) {\n      shouldRestart = true;\n      setTimeout(() => startListening(), 200);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  setTimeout(() => globalSynth?.speak(utterance), 50);\n}\n\nexport function onDigits(handler: (d: string) => void): () => void {\n  digitHandlers.add(handler);\n  return () => digitHandlers.delete(handler);\n}\n\nexport function onCommand(handler: (c: string) => void): () => void {\n  commandHandlers.add(handler);\n  return () => commandHandlers.delete(handler);\n}\n\n// React Hook\nexport function useAgenticBar() {\n  const [, forceUpdate] = useState({});\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    const listener = () => forceUpdate({});\n    listeners.add(listener);\n    initVoice();\n    return () => { listeners.delete(listener); };\n  }, []);\n  \n  return {\n    isListening: currentState === 'LISTENING',\n    isSpeaking: currentState === 'SPEAKING',\n    transcript: lastTranscript,\n    error: lastError,\n    start: startListening,\n    stop: stopListening,\n    speak\n  };\n}\n\n// Component Props\ninterface AgenticBarProps {\n  context?: string;\n  hints?: string[];\n  onDigits?: (d: string) => void;\n  onCommand?: (c: string) => void;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n  welcomeMessage?: string;\n}\n\nconst AgenticBar: React.FC<AgenticBarProps> = ({ \n  context, \n  hints, \n  onDigits: onDigitsProp, \n  onCommand: onCommandProp,\n  autoStart = true,\n  welcomeMessage\n}) => {\n  const voice = useAgenticBar();\n  const welcomeSpoken = useRef(false);\n  \n  // Register handlers\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (onDigitsProp) return onDigits(onDigitsProp);\n  }, [onDigitsProp]);\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (onCommandProp) return onCommand(onCommandProp);\n  }, [onCommandProp]);\n  \n  // Welcome message and auto-start\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!welcomeSpoken.current && welcomeMessage) {\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        speak(welcomeMessage, () => {\n          if (autoStart) startListening();\n        });\n      }, 500);\n    } else if (!welcomeSpoken.current && autoStart) {\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\n      setTimeout(() => startListening(), 500);\n    }\n  }, [welcomeMessage, autoStart]);\n  \n  const isActive = voice.isListening;\n  const statusColor = voice.isSpeaking ? '#FFD700' : isActive ? '#4CAF50' : '#f44336';\n  \n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      margin: '16px 0 0',\n      padding: '14px 16px',\n      background: isActive ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.12)' : voice.isSpeaking ? 'rgba(255,215,0,0.1)' : 'rgba(244,67,54,0.08)',\n      border: `2px solid ${statusColor}`,\n      borderRadius: '14px',\n      transition: 'all 0.3s ease'\n    }}>\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' }}>\n          <span style={{\n            width: '14px', height: '14px', borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: statusColor,\n            boxShadow: isActive ? `0 0 10px ${statusColor}` : 'none',\n            animation: isActive ? 'agbar-pulse 1.5s infinite' : 'none'\n          }} />\n          <span style={{ color: statusColor, fontWeight: 600 }}>\n            {voice.isSpeaking ? '\ud83d\udd0a Speaking...' : isActive ? '\ud83c\udfa4 Listening...' : '\u25a0 Stopped'}\n          </span>\n          {context && <span style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\u2022 {context}</span>}\n        </div>\n        \n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}>\n          {!isActive && !voice.isSpeaking ? \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport React, { useEffect, useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';\\n\\n// Word to digit mapping\\nconst W2D: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const w of words) {\\n    if (W2D[w]) digits += W2D[w];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(w)) digits += w;\\n  }\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\n// Global singleton state\\nlet globalRecognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\\nlet globalSynth: SpeechSynthesis | null = null;\\nlet isInitialized = false;\\nlet shouldRestart = true;\\nlet currentState: 'IDLE' | 'LISTENING' | 'SPEAKING' = 'IDLE';\\nconst listeners: Set<() => void> = new Set();\\nconst digitHandlers: Set<(d: string) => void> = new Set();\\nconst commandHandlers: Set<(c: string) => void> = new Set();\\nlet lastTranscript = '';\\nlet lastError: string | null = null;\\n\\nfunction notifyListeners() {\\n  listeners.forEach(l => l());\\n}\\n\\nfunction initVoice() {\\n  if (isInitialized) return;\\n  \\n  const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n  if (!SR) {\\n    lastError = 'Speech not supported. Use Chrome.';\\n    console.error('[AgenticBar] Speech not supported');\\n    return;\\n  }\\n  \\n  globalSynth = window.speechSynthesis;\\n  globalRecognition = new SR();\\n  globalRecognition.continuous = true;\\n  globalRecognition.interimResults = true;\\n  globalRecognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n  \\n  globalRecognition.onstart = () => {\\n    console.log('[AgenticBar] \\u2705 LISTENING');\\n    currentState = 'LISTENING';\\n    lastError = null;\\n    notifyListeners();\\n  };\\n  \\n  globalRecognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n    const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n    const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n    const isFinal = result.isFinal;\\n    \\n    if (isFinal && text) {\\n      console.log('[AgenticBar] Heard:', text);\\n      lastTranscript = text;\\n      notifyListeners();\\n      \\n      // Check for pause commands\\n      const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n      if (lower.includes('hey') || lower.includes('stop') || lower.includes('pause')) {\\n        stopListening();\\n        speak('Paused. Say resume to continue.');\\n        return;\\n      }\\n      if (lower.includes('resume') || lower.includes('continue')) {\\n        startListening();\\n        return;\\n      }\\n      \\n      // Dispatch digits\\n      const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n      if (digits) {\\n        digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\\n      }\\n      \\n      // Dispatch command\\n      commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(lower));\\n    }\\n  };\\n  \\n  globalRecognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n    console.log('[AgenticBar] Error:', event.error);\\n    if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n      lastError = 'Mic blocked. Click \\ud83d\\udd12 \\u2192 Allow';\\n      shouldRestart = false;\\n      currentState = 'IDLE';\\n      notifyListeners();\\n    }\\n  };\\n  \\n  globalRecognition.onend = () => {\\n    console.log('[AgenticBar] Ended, shouldRestart:', shouldRestart);\\n    if (shouldRestart && currentState !== 'SPEAKING') {\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        if (shouldRestart && globalRecognition) {\\n          try { globalRecognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n        }\\n      }, 100);\\n    } else {\\n      currentState = 'IDLE';\\n      notifyListeners();\\n    }\\n  };\\n  \\n  isInitialized = true;\\n  console.log('[AgenticBar] \\u2705 Initialized');\\n}\\n\\nexport function startListening() {\\n  initVoice();\\n  shouldRestart = true;\\n  if (globalRecognition && currentState !== 'SPEAKING') {\\n    try { globalRecognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n  }\\n}\\n\\nexport function stopListening() {\\n  shouldRestart = false;\\n  if (globalRecognition) {\\n    try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n  }\\n  currentState = 'IDLE';\\n  notifyListeners();\\n}\\n\\nexport function speak(text: string, onDone?: () => void) {\\n  if (!text) { onDone?.(); return; }\\n  \\n  initVoice();\\n  if (!globalSynth) { onDone?.(); return; }\\n  \\n  console.log('[AgenticBar] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n  \\n  // Stop listening while speaking (Audio Mutex)\\n  const wasRestarting = shouldRestart;\\n  shouldRestart = false;\\n  if (globalRecognition) {\\n    try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n  }\\n  \\n  globalSynth.cancel();\\n  currentState = 'SPEAKING';\\n  notifyListeners();\\n  \\n  const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n  utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n  utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n  utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n  \\n  const voices = globalSynth.getVoices();\\n  const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\\n  if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n  \\n  utterance.onend = () => {\\n    console.log('[AgenticBar] Speech ended');\\n    currentState = 'IDLE';\\n    notifyListeners();\\n    onDone?.();\\n    \\n    // Resume listening\\n    if (wasRestarting) {\\n      shouldRestart = true;\\n      setTimeout(() => startListening(), 200);\\n    }\\n  };\\n  \\n  utterance.onerror = () => {\\n    currentState = 'IDLE';\\n    notifyListeners();\\n    onDone?.();\\n    if (wasRestarting) {\\n      shouldRestart = true;\\n      setTimeout(() => startListening(), 200);\\n    }\\n  };\\n  \\n  setTimeout(() => globalSynth?.speak(utterance), 50);\\n}\\n\\nexport function onDigits(handler: (d: string) => void): () => void {\\n  digitHandlers.add(handler);\\n  return () => digitHandlers.delete(handler);\\n}\\n\\nexport function onCommand(handler: (c: string) => void): () => void {\\n  commandHandlers.add(handler);\\n  return () => commandHandlers.delete(handler);\\n}\\n\\n// React Hook\\nexport function useAgenticBar() {\\n  const [, forceUpdate] = useState({});\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const listener = () => forceUpdate({});\\n    listeners.add(listener);\\n    initVoice();\\n    return () => { listeners.delete(listener); };\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  return {\\n    isListening: currentState === 'LISTENING',\\n    isSpeaking: currentState === 'SPEAKING',\\n    transcript: lastTranscript,\\n    error: lastError,\\n    start: startListening,\\n    stop: stopListening,\\n    speak\\n  };\\n}\\n\\n// Component Props\\ninterface AgenticBarProps {\\n  context?: string;\\n  hints?: string[];\\n  onDigits?: (d: string) => void;\\n  onCommand?: (c: string) => void;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n  welcomeMessage?: string;\\n}\\n\\nconst AgenticBar: React.FC<AgenticBarProps> = ({ \\n  context, \\n  hints, \\n  onDigits: onDigitsProp, \\n  onCommand: onCommandProp,\\n  autoStart = true,\\n  welcomeMessage\\n}) => {\\n  const voice = useAgenticBar();\\n  const welcomeSpoken = useRef(false);\\n  \\n  // Register handlers\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (onDigitsProp) return onDigits(onDigitsProp);\\n  }, [onDigitsProp]);\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (onCommandProp) return onCommand(onCommandProp);\\n  }, [onCommandProp]);\\n  \\n  // Welcome message and auto-start\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!welcomeSpoken.current && welcomeMessage) {\\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        speak(welcomeMessage, () => {\\n          if (autoStart) startListening();\\n        });\\n      }, 500);\\n    } else if (!welcomeSpoken.current && autoStart) {\\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\\n      setTimeout(() => startListening(), 500);\\n    }\\n  }, [welcomeMessage, autoStart]);\\n  \\n  const isActive = voice.isListening;\\n  const statusColor = voice.isSpeaking ? '#FFD700' : isActive ? '#4CAF50' : '#f44336';\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <div style={{\\n      margin: '16px 0 0',\\n      padding: '14px 16px',\\n      background: isActive ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.12)' : voice.isSpeaking ? 'rgba(255,215,0,0.1)' : 'rgba(244,67,54,0.08)',\\n      border: `2px solid ${statusColor}`,\\n      borderRadius: '14px',\\n      transition: 'all 0.3s ease'\\n    }}>\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' }}>\\n          <span style={{\\n            width: '14px', height: '14px', borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: statusColor,\\n            boxShadow: isActive ? `0 0 10px ${statusColor}` : 'none',\\n            animation: isActive ? 'agbar-pulse 1.5s infinite' : 'none'\\n          }} />\\n          <span style={{ color: statusColor, fontWeight: 600 }}>\\n            {voice.isSpeaking ? '\\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking...' : isActive ? '\\ud83c\\udfa4 Listening...' : '\\u25a0 Stopped'}\\n          </span>\\n          {context && <span style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\\u2022 {context}</span>}\\n        </div>\\n        \\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}>\\n          {!isActive && !voice.isSpeaking ? VoiceState = 'IDLE' | 'LISTENING' | 'SPEAKING' | 'PAUSED' | 'THINKING';\ntype Emotion = 'neutral' | 'happy' | 'thinking' | 'concerned' | 'excited';\n\ninterface VoiceBrainState {\n  state: VoiceState;\n  transcript: string;\n  interim: string;\n  error: string | null;\n  emotion: Emotion;\n  context: string;\n  lastCommand: string;\n}\n\n// Word to digit\nconst W2D: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\n};\n\nexport function extractDigits(text: string): string {\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\s+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const w of words) {\n    if (W2D[w]) digits += W2D[w];\n    else if (/^\\d$/.test(w)) digits += w;\n  }\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\n}\n\nexport function formatPhone(d: string): string {\n  const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n}\n\nclass VoiceBrain {\n  private static instance: VoiceBrain;\n  \n  private recognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\n  private synth: SpeechSynthesis | null = null;\n  private initialized = false;\n  private shouldRestart = true;\n  \n  private state: VoiceBrainState = {\n    state: 'IDLE',\n    transcript: '',\n    interim: '',\n    error: null,\n    emotion: 'neutral',\n    context: 'home',\n    lastCommand: ''\n  };\n  \n  private listeners: Set<(s: VoiceBrainState) => void> = new Set();\n  private digitHandlers: Set<(d: string) => void> = new Set();\n  private commandHandlers: Set<(c: string) => void> = new Set();\n  private navigationHandler: ((action: string) => void) | null = null;\n  \n  private constructor() {}\n  \n  static getInstance(): VoiceBrain {\n    if (!VoiceBrain.instance) {\n      VoiceBrain.instance = new VoiceBrain();\n    }\n    return VoiceBrain.instance;\n  }\n  \n  init(): void {\n    if (this.initialized) return;\n    \n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n      this.updateState({ error: 'Speech not supported. Use Chrome.' });\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    this.synth = window.speechSynthesis;\n    this.recognition = new SR();\n    this.recognition.continuous = true;\n    this.recognition.interimResults = true;\n    this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    \n    this.recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] \u2705 LISTENING');\n      this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING', error: null });\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      const isFinal = result.isFinal;\n      \n      if (isFinal && text) {\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Heard:', text);\n        this.updateState({ transcript: text, interim: '', lastCommand: text });\n        this.processCommand(text.toLowerCase());\n      } else {\n        this.updateState({ interim: text });\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Error:', event.error);\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', error: 'Mic blocked. Click \ud83d\udd12 \u2192 Allow' });\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\n            try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else if (this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.initialized = true;\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \u2705 Initialized');\n  }\n  \n  private updateState(partial: Partial<VoiceBrainState>): void {\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\n  }\n  \n  private processCommand(text: string): void {\n    // Pause commands with empathy\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text.includes('stop') || text.includes('pause') || text.includes('wait')) {\n      this.pause();\n      this.speak(\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume or tap the button to continue.\", 'neutral');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Resume\n    if (text.includes('resume') || text.includes('continue') || text.includes('go ahead')) {\n      this.resume();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Help\n    if (text.includes('help') || text.includes('what can you do')) {\n      this.speak(\"I can help you navigate VistaView. Say things like: sign in, go back, clear, yes to confirm, or speak numbers for phone entry.\", 'happy');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Navigation commands\n    const navCommands: Record<string, string> = {\n      'sign in': 'signin', 'login': 'signin', 'log in': 'signin',\n      'vendor': 'vendor', \"i'm a vendor\": 'vendor', 'im a vendor': 'vendor',\n      'go back': 'back', 'back': 'back', 'previous': 'back',\n      'close': 'close', 'cancel': 'close', 'exit': 'close',\n      'next': 'next', 'continue': 'next', 'submit': 'next',\n      'home': 'home', 'go home': 'home',\n      'about': 'about', 'how it works': 'howitworks',\n      'partners': 'partners', 'lend': 'lend'\n    };\n    \n    for (const [phrase, action] of Object.entries(navCommands)) {\n      if (text.includes(phrase)) {\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Navigation:', action);\n        this.navigationHandler?.(action);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Extract digits\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\n    if (digits) {\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\n    }\n    \n    // Send to command handlers\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\n  }\n  \n  // Public API\n  getState(): VoiceBrainState { return this.state; }\n  \n  subscribe(listener: (s: VoiceBrainState) => void): () => void {\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\n    listener(this.state);\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\n  }\n  \n  onDigits(handler: (d: string) => void): () => void {\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n  \n  onCommand(handler: (c: string) => void): () => void {\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n  \n  setNavigationHandler(handler: (action: string) => void): void {\n    this.navigationHandler = handler;\n  }\n  \n  setContext(context: string): void {\n    this.updateState({ context });\n  }\n  \n  start(): void {\n    this.init();\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }\n  \n  stop(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\n  }\n  \n  pause(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    this.updateState({ state: 'PAUSED' });\n  }\n  \n  resume(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    this.speak(\"I'm listening.\", 'neutral');\n  }\n  \n  speak(text: string, emotion: Emotion = 'neutral', onDone?: () => void): void {\n    if (!text) { onDone?.(); return; }\n    \n    this.init();\n    if (!this.synth) { onDone?.(); return; }\n    \n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \ud83d\udd0a Speaking:', text);\n    \n    // Audio Mutex - stop listening while speaking\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    \n    this.synth.cancel();\n    this.updateState({ state: 'SPEAKING', emotion });\n    \n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    \n    // Adjust for emotion\n    switch (emotion) {\n      case 'happy':\n      case 'excited':\n        utterance.rate = 1.1; utterance.pitch = 1.1; break;\n      case 'concerned':\n        utterance.rate = 0.9; utterance.pitch = 0.9; break;\n      case 'thinking':\n        utterance.rate = 0.85; break;\n      default:\n        utterance.rate = 1.0; utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    }\n    \n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n    \n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n    \n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      this.updateState({ state: wasListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\n      onDone?.();\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    utterance.onerror = () => {\n      this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\n      onDone?.();\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    setTimeout(() => this.synth?.speak(utterance), 50);\n  }\n  \n  stopSpeaking(): void {\n    this.synth?.cancel();\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', Use Chrome.' });\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    this.synth = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    this.recognition = new SR();\\n    this.recognition.continuous = true;\\n    this.recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\u2705 LISTENING');\\n      this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING', error: null });\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      const isFinal = result.isFinal;\\n      \\n      if (isFinal && text) {\\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Heard:', text);\\n        this.updateState({ transcript: text, interim: '', lastCommand: text });\\n        this.processCommand(text.toLowerCase());\\n      } else {\\n        this.updateState({ interim: text });\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', error: 'Mic blocked. Click \\ud83d\\udd12 \\u2192 Allow' });\\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\\n            try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else if (this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.initialized = true;\\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\u2705 Initialized');\\n  }\\n  \\n  private updateState(partial: Partial<VoiceBrainState>): void {\\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\\n  }\\n  \\n  private processCommand(text: string): void {\\n    // Pause commands with empathy\\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text.includes('stop') || text.includes('pause') || text.includes('wait')) {\\n      this.pause();\\n      this.speak(\\\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume or tap the button to continue.\\\", 'neutral');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Resume\\n    if (text.includes('resume') || text.includes('continue') || text.includes('go ahead')) {\\n      this.resume();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Help\\n    if (text.includes('help') || text.includes('what can you do')) {\\n      this.speak(\\\"I can help you navigate VistaView. Say things like: sign in, go back, clear, yes to confirm, or speak numbers for phone entry.\\\", 'happy');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Navigation commands\\n    const navCommands: Record<string, string> = {\\n      'sign in': 'signin', 'login': 'signin', 'log in': 'signin',\\n      'vendor': 'vendor', \\\"i'm a vendor\\\": 'vendor', 'im a vendor': 'vendor',\\n      'go back': 'back', 'back': 'back', 'previous': 'back',\\n      'close': 'close', 'cancel': 'close', 'exit': 'close',\\n      'next': 'next', 'continue': 'next', 'submit': 'next',\\n      'home': 'home', 'go home': 'home',\\n      'about': 'about', 'how it works': 'howitworks',\\n      'partners': 'partners', 'lend': 'lend'\\n    };\\n    \\n    for (const [phrase, action] of Object.entries(navCommands)) {\\n      if (text.includes(phrase)) {\\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Navigation:', action);\\n        this.navigationHandler?.(action);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract digits\\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n    if (digits) {\\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Send to command handlers\\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\\n  }\\n  \\n  // Public API\\n  getState(): VoiceBrainState { return this.state; }\\n  \\n  subscribe(listener: (s: VoiceBrainState) => void): () => void {\\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\\n    listener(this.state);\\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\\n  }\\n  \\n  onDigits(handler: (d: string) => void): () => void {\\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\\n  }\\n  \\n  onCommand(handler: (c: string) => void): () => void {\\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\\n  }\\n  \\n  setNavigationHandler(handler: (action: string) => void): void {\\n    this.navigationHandler = handler;\\n  }\\n  \\n  setContext(context: string): void {\\n    this.updateState({ context });\\n  }\\n  \\n  start(): void {\\n    this.init();\\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  stop(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\\n  }\\n  \\n  pause(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'PAUSED' });\\n  }\\n  \\n  resume(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.speak(\\\"I'm listening.\\\", 'neutral');\\n  }\\n  \\n  speak(text: string, emotion: Emotion = 'neutral', onDone?: () => void): void {\\n    if (!text) { onDone?.(); return; }\\n    \\n    this.init();\\n    if (!this.synth) { onDone?.(); return; }\\n    \\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n    \\n    // Audio Mutex - stop listening while speaking\\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    this.synth.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'SPEAKING', emotion });\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    \\n    // Adjust for emotion\\n    switch (emotion) {\\n      case 'happy':\\n      case 'excited':\\n        utterance.rate = 1.1; utterance.pitch = 1.1; break;\\n      case 'concerned':\\n        utterance.rate = 0.9; utterance.pitch = 0.9; break;\\n      case 'thinking':\\n        utterance.rate = 0.85; break;\\n      default:\\n        utterance.rate = 1.0; utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    }\\n    \\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n    \\n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n    \\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      this.updateState({ state: wasListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\\n      onDone?.();\\n      if (wasListening) {\\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    utterance.onerror = () => {\\n      this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\\n      onDone?.();\\n      if (wasListening) {\\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => this.synth?.speak(utterance), 50);\\n  }\\n  \\n  stopSpeaking(): void {\\n    this.synth?.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\\n  }\\n}\\n\\n// Export singleton\\nexport const voiceBrain = VoiceBrain.getInstance();\\nexport default voiceBrain;\\nBRAINEOF\\n\\necho \\\"
